○000289○The first slice was delicious.

○000290○But after that, the thought that every one of the remaining seven slices would taste the same sunk my spirits into the gutter...
●000290●但是在那之后，一想到其他七块披萨都是这个味道，心情不由得就郁闷了起来…。

○000291○Not to mention it was rapidly cooling off, so they'd actually taste worse...
●000291●而且很快就凉了下来，味道也变差了…。

○000292○Ask Hinata for help
